Local News

Typhoon Warning in Shanghai 118

All Sea Vessels Suspended

Yesterday, due to the impending typhoon in Shanghai, the Observatory and the Jianghai Customs fired cannons after 4:00 PM to notify all shipping companies to take precautions, resulting in the complete suspension of coastal shipping. Details of the investigation are as follows:

Observatory Issues Warning The Xujiahui Observatory issued a special alert yesterday at 11:00 AM, stating that the typhoon had clearly spread to northern Zhejiang and the Ningbo area, with severe cyclones in the Ma'anshan area. It is reported that the wind is coming from 123 degrees east longitude and 27 degrees north latitude, proceeding northwest-west from the islands south of Ryukyu. Yesterday morning, the typhoon passed over the Wenzhou waters with strong force, and there were also heavy rains. A reporter met with Mr. Wang, a Chinese maritime expert, who said that he had observed the weather and climate, and if the wind direction remained unchanged, it was expected to reach Shanghai around 1:00 AM this morning. Mr. Wang also said that the slight rain yesterday afternoon was a forecast of the approaching typhoon. Mr. Wang has been the owner of ocean-going vessels for more than ten years, and his words seem credible.

Warning Ball and Cannons Sounded Yesterday afternoon around 4:00 PM, a large black warning ball was raised high on the climate platform of the Observatory at the eastern end of Avenue Edward VII along the Huangpu River, and multiple wind warning signals were hung on both sides to notify commercial vessels sailing on the river. At 4:35 PM, the Jianghai Customs' flag platform at Lujiazui in Pudong also raised a large black warning ball on the top of the platform, and simultaneously fired a warning cannon to alert the shipping community to take precautions in advance. Barges, small boats, sampans, ferries, and other vessels in the Huangpu River immediately berthed at the docks or sailed into the inner harbor to prevent capsizing.

Ningbo Ships Suspended Around 4:00 PM yesterday afternoon, China Merchants Sanbei received telegrams from the Ningbo Xin Jiangtian and Ningxing vessels, stating that they were unable to depart from Ningbo due to typhoon avoidance and were currently staying in Ningbo. In addition, Taikoo's Xin Beijing, Ningshao, and Xin Ningshao were scheduled to depart for Ningbo yesterday. After receiving warnings from the Observatory and the Customs, they announced the suspension of one sailing and issued a notice to reschedule the departure for tomorrow. Passengers who had already boarded the ships received refunds and disembarked one after another, returning to their respective destinations.

Wenzhou Ships Sheltering From Wind The Shanghai-Taiwan and Wenzhou-bound vessels, including the Zhoushan, were also temporarily suspended yesterday, and the announcement was extended for one day. The China Merchants Bureau's Wenzhou-bound vessel Jiahe, which departed from Shanghai the day before yesterday, encountered strong winds before reaching Wenzhou. According to a telegram from the vessel yesterday, it had temporarily stopped in the middle of the journey to avoid the wind and was not in danger.

Coastal Vessels Delayed All coastal commercial vessels scheduled to depart this morning, such as Taikoo's Xinjiang and Yichang, were bound for Nanhua ports in Shantou, Xiamen, and Guangdong, which are on the inevitable path of the typhoon. Yesterday, the company had already extended the departure date of each vessel by one day. Those that had already departed were notified by the vessel bureaus via radio to anchor at the Wusongkou to temporarily avoid going out to sea to avoid danger. Vessels entering the port, on the other hand, were expedited to sail into the Huangpu River.

Small Boats in the Huangpu River Take Precautions Yesterday afternoon from 5:00 PM, cargo barges, ferries, and other small boats on the Huangpu River had already suspended operations early. Private boats that had unloaded their cargo at the docks sailed into the Suzhou Creek to take temporary shelter. Therefore, there were no ships sailing on the river in the evening. However, Yangtze River vessels, which do not pass through the sea route, still planned to depart.

City Party Headquarters Declaration 119

Opposing the Swiss Consul's Protection of Communists

The Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Nationalist Party declared: "The greatest disaster in our country at present is none other than the Red bandits, and the most important task in our country at present is none other than to eliminate the Red bandits. The scourge of the Red bandits is not only sufficient to overthrow our country's political system and destroy our country's society, but also sufficient to cut off the livelihood of our people, eliminate the population of our country, and endanger the survival of our race. The spread of the Red scourge in Jiangxi, Hunan, and other places is already waning and gradually being eliminated, but its lurking in other places is still restless, plotting to make a move, and cannot be ignored by us. This city is located in a strategic location and has long been coveted by the Red bandits, especially with the concessions serving as a barrier for their actions. Therefore, most of the important members of the Red bandits are hiding here to plan their work of murder and arson. In early June of this year, the head of the Eastern Department of the Third International, the Russian couple Noulens, were hiding in the Public Concession and were uncovered by the police. The Noulens were arrested together, and hundreds of important pieces of evidence were seized, including plans to command the Red Army in combat and the use of poison gas, which were shocking to read. During the interrogation of the criminals, Noulens claimed to be Belgian, and his wife claimed to be French. Later, after inquiries were made by the authorities, it was found that everything was false. The current government sent a letter to the court requesting extradition. On the 7th of this month, the date of the court hearing, the court ruled that the crimes committed were entirely to disrupt the peace of the Chinese mainland, and the tragedies of the Red bandits' murder and arson were all instructed by Noulens. Moreover, the nationality he claimed had long been denied by Belgium, so the extradition was approved according to law. The Garrison Headquarters immediately sent personnel to take custody, but unexpectedly, the Swiss Consul suddenly sent a letter to the police, admitting that the criminal was a Swiss national and opposing the transfer. However, after investigation, the criminal claimed to be Belgian and then Swiss, which is contradictory and shows that his claim is false. Although the Swiss Consul admitted that the criminal was Swiss, the criminal had never registered in Switzerland, nor did he have a Swiss passport, nor did he have any evidence to prove his Swiss nationality. The evidence that he colluded with the criminal to protect the Communist Party is conclusive, and the responsibility lies with him. In addition to presenting a note to the central government to severely reprimand the Swiss Minister, we now issue a declaration on the course of events so that our citizens will know the absurdity of the Swiss Consul. He is indeed greedy for undue gain and is willing to act as a henchman for Red Russia, to slaughter the people of our China and destroy the organization of our Chinese society. His intention is absurd, and his actions are wrong, as well as the scourge of the concessions and consular jurisdiction, and we must think of ways to correct them. We hope that all citizens will rise up together, and it will be fortunate."

The Presidents of the High Court and Second Special Court

Swore Oaths Yesterday 120

Supervised by Su Xixun from the Ministry and Tong Xingbai from the Party

Guests Included Wang Yansong and Yuan Ludeng, who Gave Speeches

The two new courts, the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court and the Shanghai Second Special District Local Court, which were announced to be established on the 1st of this month, had their presidents and chief prosecutors, as well as all the staff, complete the supplementary oath-taking ceremony in the criminal court of the court on Avenue Guynemer in the French Concession at 10:00 AM yesterday. In addition to Su Xixun, the chief of the General Affairs Section dispatched by the Judicial Yuan of the National Government's Administrative Department, and Tong Xingbai, dispatched by the Shanghai Special City Party Department, attending the ceremony to supervise the oath, representatives from various Chinese and foreign institutions and communities in Shanghai were also sent to participate. The details of yesterday's ceremony are recorded below:

Guests Present Yesterday, many guests from various Chinese and foreign circles attended, including Geng Jiaji, Secretary of the Municipal Government; Xu Weizhen, President of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court; Yang Zhaoyun, President of the Shanghai First Special District Local Court; Cai Zengji, Director of the Finance Bureau; Xu Peihuang, Director of the Education Bureau; Chen Xizeng, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau; Jiang Yi, representative of the Garrison Headquarters; Zhan Jifeng, Legal Counsel; Yuan Ludeng, Chinese Director of the Public Concession Bureau; Zhong E, Director of the Telecommunications Administration; Wang Yansong, representative of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; foreign guests included Duge, Advisor to the Second Special District Local Court; Gadant, French Vice Consul; Fei, Chief Inspector of the French Police; Kennett, representative of the Public Concession Bureau; Wei Yinde, Deputy Secretary; and many staff members from the two courts.

Ceremony Details At 10:10 AM, the meeting was announced to be open, presided over by President Liang Renjie, with Su Jinglin as the master of ceremonies, and Tang Zaili and Xiao Jinfang as receptionists. After all the oath-takers took the oath in accordance with the ceremony, Su Xixun, the oath supervisor dispatched by the Judicial Administrative Department, and Tong Xingbai, the representative of the Municipal Party Department of the Headquarters, delivered speeches successively. Then, Wang Yansong and Yuan Ludeng gave speeches. At around 11:00 AM, the chairman gave a reply, and the ceremony was announced to be over. Photos were taken, and tea and refreshments were served.

Oath Takers Liang Renjie, President of the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court; Peng Wangye, Chief Prosecutor; Tang Zaili, Chief Secretary; and all judges and staff of various departments; Ying Shi, President of the Shanghai Second Special District Local Court; Chen Beisan, Chief Prosecutor; Xiao Jinfang, Chief Clerk; and the warden, all judges, and staff of various departments.

Group Photo of the Oath-Taking Ceremony for the High Court and Second Special Court (Photo by this Newspaper) 121

Original Text of the Oath The original text of the oath sworn by the presidents, etc., reads: "I solemnly swear that I will strictly abide by the teachings of the Premier, obey the party's righteousness, abide by the laws, and be loyal and diligent in my duties. I will never waste a penny or misuse a person, and I will never engage in embezzlement or bribery. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment. This oath."

Ying Shi (Photo by this Newspaper) Liang Renjie 122

Oath Supervisor's Speech First, Su Xixun, the representative of the Judicial Yuan and oath supervisor, gave a speech, stating: "Today, I am very honored and pleased to be here as a representative to participate in the oath-taking ceremony of the two presidents. The greatest goal of this recovery of the French Concession is, on the one hand, to implement the recovery of judicial power, and on the other hand, to complete the unification of judicial power. Now, through diplomatic efforts and the backing of the people, the abnormal organization that has hindered judicial power for eighty years has been abolished, and two local courts of the Republic of China have been established. The recovery of judicial power has been realized, and the unification of judicial power has been completed. However, the Judicial Yuan has two points to convey to you: (1) The two courts themselves, in the initial stage of their establishment, should consider all facilities, measures, and matters that should be promoted and reformed in a comprehensive manner to achieve perfection. However, at the beginning, it is inevitable that things will be slightly difficult, so you must carefully consider the advantages and disadvantages and be cautious in your actions to gradually improve and solve all difficulties. (2) To meet the wishes of the general public, you must have better results. The quality of the results depends on the degree of effort. For example, if the score is 100 points as the standard, if you can reach 90 points, then the results are excellent. If you do not reach half of the points, then you still need to work harder. I hope that all of you in the two courts will put in your best efforts and strive to make the future of the courts a very good one to show the spirit of the Republic of China's legislation. According to my personal feelings, the two presidents and all of you in the two courts are knowledgeable and experienced. In the future, you will definitely live up to the expectations of the government and the people, and I can congratulate you on your success in advance."

Party Representative's Speech Tong Xingbai, the representative of the Municipal Party Department, said: "Today, I am attending the oath-taking ceremony of the two courts, and at the same time, I am filled with a deep sense of sorrow in this very happy occasion. The land, the people, and sovereignty are the essential elements of the national spirit of any country. Why does our country have this unhealthy disease? Of course, it is because of the imperialists' seizure of power. At the same time, we should look back at the past suffering and work doubly hard. In the eyes of the general public, the oath seems to be completely a formality, but the Premier considered it to be the most important task at the time. Therefore, holding the oath is to implement one of the Premier's teachings, and the oath-takers should also take this as a warning and self-encouragement. There are still a few points that I would like to offer to you: (1) Law, judges must have a basis and responsibility. If you violate the oath, you will inevitably be held responsible. (2) Morality, judges should not only be held legally responsible but also pay attention to moral issues. I know that the judges of the two courts have always been highly regarded, and they will definitely have good results in the future. (3) In the past, the French Concession Court was unable to be rectified due to foreign constraints and diplomatic restraints. This kind of pain will definitely be reduced after the recovery, and all rectifications can be carried out. Although there may be accumulated problems that cannot be solved at once, all necessary reforms should be made as much as possible."

Guests' Speeches Wang Yansong, the representative of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, said: "This time, the abolition of the French Concession Court and the establishment of the Chinese-style court is a cause for celebration. From now on, the residents of the French Concession will have the guarantee of the 'law.' The current judges are all knowledgeable and experienced, and with their integrity and impartiality, it is expected that the future results will be remarkable. The realization of the entire recovery of judicial power should be the starting point for this. This is not only the good fortune of the business community but also the common expectation of the people of the whole country." The rest is omitted.

Chairman's Reply Chairman Liang Renjie replied: "Today, we are honored that the Judicial Yuan, the Municipal Party Department, and representatives from all walks of life have come to supervise and guide us. All the members of the two courts are extremely honored. We will sincerely accept the instructions of all the representatives. We are all lacking in talent and shallow in learning. Since taking office, we have been cautious and fearful of making mistakes. From now on, we feel that the responsibility is even greater both internally and externally. We can only abide by the oath and uphold the three principles of integrity, prudence, and diligence and work hard. If there is anything inappropriate, we still hope that all walks of life will give us guidance."

After the Registration of Japanese Goods is Completed

Detailed Rules for Passage are Defined 123

Yu Qiaqing Attends the Standing Committee Meeting

A Decision is Made to Set Up a Branch Office in Wusong

After the Anti-Japanese Aid to Overseas Chinese Committee completed its registration, the detailed rules for the passage of Japanese goods that had been detained after completing the supplementary registration and paying the money, as well as the investigation procedures, were all approved by the Executive Committee and will be implemented immediately. The committee also held a Standing Committee meeting yesterday, which was attended by Standing Committee member Yu Qiaqing. A decision was made to set up a branch office in Wusong, and the director and deputy director of the branch office were appointed. The various news items are recorded below:

Detailed Rules for Passage The committee has stipulated the following detailed rules for the registration of Japanese goods and the payment of money for the passage of goods that were detained for smuggling without following the public registration procedures: (1) The Japanese goods merchant must fill out three "registration forms" at the registration section. (2) After the registration section receives the registration form, it will distribute it as follows: (a) One copy will be kept for record; (b) One copy will be sent to the investigation section; (c) One copy will be sent to the secretariat. (3) When the registration section sends the above form to the investigation section, it must also attach a signed list of the personnel involved, which must be sealed by the director and staff of the registration section. (4) After the investigation section receives the two forms and one list sent by the registration section, it must immediately send personnel to investigate and fill out the "Registration Goods Investigation Report Form," sending one copy to the secretariat (along with the signed list of the personnel involved), one copy to the registration section, and keeping one copy for record. (5) After the secretariat receives the registration form, etc., from the registration section and the "Investigation Report Form" and "Signed List of Personnel Involved" from the investigation section, it must immediately fill out the "Notice of Payment of Relief Funds" and the "Notice of Withdrawal," notifying the merchant and simultaneously making a duplicate copy to notify the accounting department. If the investigation situation is inconsistent, the merchant should be notified to re-register. (6) After receiving the notice, the merchant should immediately deposit the money at the bank designated by the committee, obtain a receipt, and then go to the accounting department of the committee to verify the amount. If it is correct, the accounting department will stamp "Verified Correct" and return it to the secretariat, which will notify the registration section to issue a passage permit. (7) If the goods are in the possession of the committee, the secretariat should immediately notify the storage section to release them. These detailed rules specifically refer to detained goods. Those who come to the committee to request registration in accordance with the law and pay for the goods that were purchased before July 14 will not be charged, that is, they do not need to pay the money.

Investigation Procedures The committee's procedures for investigating detained Japanese goods are as follows: (1) The investigation section may jointly investigate the detained Japanese goods with the inspection section. (2) When investigation is needed, it may inspect the goods together with the owner. (3) After the investigation, it must be filled out in detail in accordance with the investigation report form. (4) After the investigation, a "Checked" symbol will be affixed to the goods, and the same number will be compiled according to the investigation report form number, and then the investigator will sign. (5) During the investigation, if it is found that the goods are definitely not Japanese goods, it must also be stated in the detailed column of the investigation report form what country's goods they are. (6) The investigation report form that has been filled out each day must be compiled and submitted to the director of the section for review.

Standing Committee Meeting The committee held its eighth Standing Committee meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday, which was attended by committee members Yu Qiaqing, Wang Yansong, Lu Jingshi, Tao Baichuan, and Hou Dachun. Wang Yansong was elected as chairman, and Xue Guangqian was the recorder. The important matters resolved are as follows: (1) It was discussed that the relief funds that should be taken from the detained goods should be fully used for the case of aiding and relieving overseas Chinese. Resolution: Passed. (2) It was discussed that the Executive Committee referred the case of organizing a branch office in Wusong. Resolution: To organize the Wusong Branch Office of the Shanghai Municipal Anti-Japanese Aid to Overseas Chinese Committee, appoint Sun Mingqi as the director, and Cheng Kuanzheng as the deputy director, and report to the next Executive Committee. (3) It was discussed that the inspection section proposed the case of Pu Wenbin, the manager of Xinhua Factory, fabricating news and reversing right and wrong. Resolution: Handed over to the investigation section. (4) It was discussed that the cases of releasing various goods. Resolution: Released separately. (5) It was discussed that the cases of passing various goods. Resolution: Passed separately. (6) It was discussed that the investigation section reported that the Zhen Da Haiwei Firm had detained one piece of so-called Western shark fin, and the Zhen Taihao Firm had detained five pieces of unlicensed fine cloth, which were indeed Japanese goods. Resolution: Should be detained.

Japanese Goods Samples The committee received a telegram from the Nanchang Municipal Various Industries Guild's Economic Isolation Support Association for Japan, which said: "The world's telegram counts, our association has started to register enemy goods from today, but there are many names for enemy goods, and it is not easy to identify them. Now we telegram you again, please send a copy of the enemy goods samples as soon as possible for our reference." The committee immediately replied by letter, saying: "Dear Sir, we have received your telegram requesting us to send a copy of the enemy goods samples, etc. We are currently investigating the samples. Once we have investigated and compiled them, we will send them to you."

A New Discovery in the Treatment of Tuberculosis

Translated from the German Tuberculosis Sanatorium Magazine 125

What is the Tuberculosis Bacterium? 126

The tubercle bacillus (i.e., tuberculosis bacterium) is a rod-shaped bacterium. Its body is straight or slightly curved. Its length is approximately one and a half millionths of a meter, which is invisible to the naked eye. According to a certain method, using skillful means, a stained specimen is prepared and examined under a microscope with a magnification of 600 to 1,000 times. Only then can it be seen. It is indeed an extremely small thing.

In ancient times, China called it the "consumption cough worm." Today, people all know that the tubercle bacillus is the worm of tuberculosis, but it does not belong to the animal kingdom. There are countless lower microorganisms existing around us, commonly known as minute organisms, which are invisible to the naked eye. These minute organisms are divided into two types: animal and plant. Those belonging to the animal type are called protozoa, and those belonging to the plant type are called molds. These lower plant molds belong to a family of cryptogams and have no chlorophyll. Molds are further divided into three types according to their shape and quality: "filamentous molds," "budding molds," and "fission molds."

The Colonial Policy of Tuberculosis Bacteria 127

The reproduction of fission molds is based on their own fission action, that is, changing from one to two, and from two to four, gradually increasing. Therefore, they are called fission molds. Humans and other animals often develop diseases because of them. Therefore, they are called "pathogenic bacteria." They are further divided into three types according to their different shapes: "spherical molds," "rod-shaped molds," and "spiral molds." The tuberculosis bacterium is a rod-shaped bacterium in the fission mold.

Tuberculosis bacteria are most abundant in the sputum of tuberculosis patients. They often increase or decrease depending on the severity of the patient's condition. According to Dr. Haekler of Cape Ray, Germany, a piece of sputum from a tuberculosis patient contains 300 million tubercle bacilli. Therefore, a person who coughs up sputum once per hour has 7.2 billion tubercle bacilli excreted from the body of the tuberculosis patient and spread into the air. People in the world are attacked by them day and night. But where do these many pathogenic bacteria come from? The main body of fission bacteria has a fission function, as mentioned above. They gradually increase and multiply. That is why. At the beginning, it was originally a mold. Later, it gradually split, from one to two, and from two to four, and so on. The force of proliferation gradually expanded. Now, let's assume that the rate of proliferation is that the fission function is performed once every small amount. Then, within 24 hours, one mold has turned into 16 million. From this point of view, the following matters can be inferred:

(1) How vigorous is the reproductive power of mold bacteria?

(2) Why do countless pathogenic bacteria occur in the patient's body?

(3) Why does the patient's sputum contain countless tubercle bacilli?

The Resistance of Tuberculosis Bacteria 128

The resistance of tubercle bacilli is extremely strong. Ascertaining the magnitude of its resistance is of utmost importance for the prevention and treatment of tuberculosis. When the sputum of tuberculosis patients is left in the air, the survival of tubercle bacilli can last for more than half a year. If placed in a dark room lacking light, they can still survive for more than a year. These bacteria are particularly resistant to cold. They can withstand temperatures as low as minus 10 degrees Celsius for six or seven weeks without dying. Their resistance to heat is also stronger than that of other bacteria. Other bacteria die after being exposed to a temperature of 60 degrees Celsius for 20 to 30 minutes, while these bacteria require a temperature of 80 degrees Celsius for 20 to 30 minutes to be killed. However, their resistance to sunlight is very weak. They die after being exposed to direct sunlight for five to six minutes, and they die after being exposed to heat of 100 degrees Celsius or higher for one to two minutes. In terms of disinfectants, tubercle bacilli from tuberculosis patients die in 20 times concentrated carbolic acid water in 30 seconds, in 100 times concentrated carbolic acid water in one minute, and in 1000 times concentrated mercuric chloride water in ten minutes.

Figure Eighty-Two: Physiological X-Ray Image of the Lungs Produced by Dr. Asemann of Germany 129

Dewaxing and Killing Method for Tuberculosis Bacteria 130

The cause of pulmonary tuberculosis (i.e., consumption) is the tubercle bacillus. Once this bacterium enters the human body, it forms nodules at that location, cutting off the blood supply. Furthermore, the tubercle bacillus can secrete an acid-fast waxy substance that surrounds its body to defend against the invasion of all external medicinal forces. Therefore, even with various antibacterial drugs administered internally or by injection, they ultimately cannot reach the substance of the bacteria. The natural therapies, symptomatic therapies, physical therapies, serum therapies, pharmaceutical therapies, and all other treatments that physicians have traditionally used have not been entirely successful. The saying that there is no cure for tuberculosis has been widespread because the profound principle was not known. Therefore, modern tuberculosis scholars, based on the above theory, continue to research tirelessly. As a result, they have created this chemical panacea for completely killing tubercle bacilli, called Sanosn. This medicine was successfully invented based on the latest medical theories of Dr. Koch of Germany, the discoverer of tubercle bacilli, and Dr. Berger of Germany, the inventor of the tubercle bacillus dewaxing technique. According to experimental reports from various tuberculosis sanatoriums in Germany, Switzerland, and other countries, this medicine has the effect of penetrating the nodules of the pulmonary lesions and dissolving the waxy substance. It has bactericidal power and can radically cure tuberculosis in stages one, two, and three, with truly effective results. In China, the Central Hygiene Laboratory of the National Government has tested it and found that the medicine is mild in nature, non-toxic, and has absolutely no side effects. A brief summary of its therapeutic effects is as follows:

(1) When testing the medicinal power of "Sanosn" in a test tube, after one minute, all tubercle bacilli are completely killed, without exception.

(2) According to animal experiments, it was discovered that "Sanosn" can penetrate the tuberculosis lesion. Examination of the tubercle bacilli lurking within the lesion revealed that they have completely lost their acid-fastness. This sufficiently proves that their waxy substance has been completely dissolved.

(3) If patients take "Sanosn" internally for about a week, a noticeable improvement in their condition will be observed, such as thinning of sputum and a decrease in body temperature.

(4) Continuing to take "Sanosn" internally for 30 to 60 days or more will result in a significant increase in body weight, increased appetite, and gradual alleviation of all symptoms, ultimately achieving the miraculous effect of recovery.

A complimentary Sanosn experimental report and tuberculosis care guide will be sent upon request. 131

Reply to the Hangzhou Chamber of Commerce: The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce explains that Japanese goods registered in accordance with the law do not incur fees in accordance with the regulations of the Anti-Japanese Association. The collection of relief funds is limited only to Japanese goods purchased after the 14th and before the 24th, and those that have not followed the registration procedures and are directly reported for transportation, and are therefore detained. The original letter stated that the letter received from Zhanlai on the 8th of this month requested that the Anti-Japanese Association be notified to return all industrial and commercial imports before the establishment of the association and release them without restriction. The Anti-Japanese Association had already published a public announcement on the steps to deal with Japanese goods. The first item of A stipulates that Japanese goods purchased by merchants before July 14th should be registered with the association within the registration deadline. After the registration period expires, certificates will be issued to allow them to be sold without charge. Therefore, the statement in the letter that "Japanese goods before the 14th, registered according to law, must donate 10%" is not specified in the association's announcement. It is unknown what the Knitting Industry Association of your city is based on. As for the statement in your association that "imports from various factories before the establishment of the Anti-Japanese Association should be released without restriction," the first item of Article A stipulated by the association is handled in this way. However, the registration procedure is indispensable, otherwise, how would it be known whether it was purchased before the 14th or after the 14th? Therefore, registration without charge is what your association calls unrestricted release. As for Japanese goods purchased with silver before July 14th that have not been registered and are reported for transport and sale, those that have been discovered by the Anti-Japanese Association should be levied a relief fund of 10% and supplemented with registration, etc., because before registration, the movement of Japanese goods was stopped. The Anti-Japanese Association had already announced this, but the merchants still ignored it and continued to transport and sell them. It cannot be said that they were taking advantage of the opportunity to avoid registration. Therefore, the treatment method cannot but be slightly different from those who purchased and stored silver before July 14th and did not move it. As for Japanese goods purchased with silver after July 14th and before July 24th, the Anti-Japanese Association had already been established at that time, and an economic severance with Japan had already been decided. The knitting industry association in your city also believes that it should be punished after the leadership of the group. Therefore, there is a method of collecting 10% or 20% of the fund depending on whether it is registered or not. The original letter from the knitting industry association in your city already stated that it should be punished, but suddenly pointed out that the method of adding the fund was an increase in cost out of thin air, expressing dissent. The arguments before and after are inevitably inconsistent. Summarizing the above situation, there are those that are completely misreported, such as saying that "registration before the 14th according to law, a fee of 10%, and those that have been shipped and seized will be charged 20%," and those whose own arguments are inconsistent. There is no need to send another letter to the Anti-Japanese Association. A detailed explanation is hereby made, hoping that you will check and forward it.

First half of the year

China's Trade Surplus with Japan 132

Report from the Japanese Commercial Officer

Rare in trade history

The office of the Japanese Commercial Consul in Shanghai received a telegram from the Ministry of Commerce in Japan yesterday, stating that Japan's export trade in July was worth 10.03 million Japanese yen, and compared with import trade, there was a surplus of 9 million yen. However, the results of foreign trade in the first seven months of this year show a total import surplus of 10.03 million yen, which is slightly less than the import surplus of 10.07 million yen in the same period last year. In addition, the status of Japan's foreign trade with major countries in the first half of this year is as follows: exports to the United States are worth 19.5 million yuan, resulting in a surplus of 4.8 million yuan; exports to China are worth 14 million yuan, resulting in a deficit of 1.9 million yuan (according to China, this is a trade surplus with Japan, a rare phenomenon in Sino-Japanese trade); exports to India are worth 57 million yuan, resulting in a deficit of 32 million yuan.

Dancer and Sailor 141

Interesting Anecdotes of Passionate Love 142

Sailor returns home...dancer suddenly on board

Dancer is expelled...sailor drowns in the sea

Avenue Joffre...two people meet with joy

The Great American Evening Post reported that there was a pair of dance partners in the New Victoria bar. The man was Duencun, a sailor on the Bardohong steamer, and the woman was Xie Liefusijia Ya, an 18-year-old girl living at 516 Avenue Joffre. The two were deeply in love and danced until midnight. Before long, the Bardohong set sail and headed for Seattle across the Pacific Ocean. On Friday afternoon last week, when the ship entered the sea, Xie was suddenly found in Du's cabin. Because she did not want to taste the pain of parting, she secretly boarded the ship to go to the United States with him. However, she was discovered by her colleagues, and she was returned to the ship and forcibly sent ashore at Wusong, and a telegram was sent to the manager of the company in Shanghai to send someone to accompany her back to Shanghai. Then, she turned her helm to the east again. Unexpectedly, after a few hours, Duencun was reported missing again. A thorough search of the ship found nothing. Until seventeen hours later, the Japanese ship Zhaoguo Maru passed by and caught sight of a person in the sea. It quickly released a small boat to rescue him, and it turned out to be Du. When asked about the reason, he said that he secretly carried a life jacket and jumped into the sea when the ship left Wusong, wanting to swim ashore to follow his lover. Unexpectedly, the tide receded and the water was rapid, and he drifted into the sea. He was rescued by the Japanese ship near a buoy sixty miles away and handed over to the caretaker of the buoy, who entrusted a German ship to carry him back to Shanghai. He arrived in port yesterday and was notified by the water patrol to the US Patrol Station to send someone to escort him ashore. After questioning, he was released because there was no specific article of law. After Du left the US Patrol Station, he quickly walked to the French Concession and met his lover in a room on Avenue Joffre with joy. He now hopes to find a place to stay in Shanghai so that he can discuss marriage with Xie.

Woman from Haimen

Accuses the owner of Qinglian Pavilion 143

The statements in the lawsuit are extremely dirty

Beaten and injured, requests punishment

Sun Yunqing (i.e., Sun Shaorui), the owner of Qinglian Pavilion Teahouse at the intersection of Fuzhou Road and Hubei Road, a local person, is over sixty years old and lives at No. 16 Yuyuan Road, West Shanghai. Recently, Jiang Cuiling, a 26-year-old woman from Haimen, hired lawyer Chen Bingxing to sue him for injury in the First Special District Court. The gist of the lawsuit is extracted as follows: It is a matter of requesting punishment according to law for being punched, injured, and coughing up blood. I, the plaintiff, was originally a woman from a good family. I came to Shanghai when I was young and lived with my relatives. Unexpectedly, I was lured and sold by a villain to the defendant's home as a maid. At that time, the plaintiff's parents came to Shanghai and learned of the situation. They reported it to the former Mixed Court, and the villain was sentenced to imprisonment. After the case was settled, the plaintiff's father wanted to take her back, but the defendant repeatedly dissuaded him and asked her to stay there. He agreed to it. How could he know that the defendant was a beast in human clothing, without humanity, and actually used violent and coercive means to commit indecency. At that time, the plaintiff was young and ignorant, had no strength to resist, and it was a matter of face, so she dared not publicize it and endured humiliation for several years. During these several years, she suffered all kinds of abuse. For example, in April of last year, she was punched in the chest by the defendant, causing her to breathe painfully and cough up blood. The plaintiff originally wanted to sue him for the crime, but she was persuaded by many parties to stop. However, the plaintiff suffered this blow and was bedridden for more than a month. She was treated by Chinese medicine doctor Wang Zhongqi, and the coughing up of blood stopped. However, there is still pain in her chest today. Especially when the defendant was sick, his ambition did not diminish, and he wanted to have sex with her. If he did not comply, he would be threatened. This kind of behavior is really devoid of conscience. However, the defendant bullies the weak by relying on his strength, and it is getting worse day by day. On July 21 of this year, the plaintiff was in her menstrual period, but the defendant insisted on his lust and forced her to have sex. The plaintiff refused politely, which aroused his anger. On the 22nd of this month, he dared to beat the plaintiff with old fists on the pretext of beating the plaintiff, injuring her shoulders, waist, chest, etc. At that time, she coughed up several mouthfuls of blood, and there were people present who witnessed it. This kind of tragic situation was treated by Dr. Chen Xingzhen and is currently taking medicine. It is found that the defendant has repeatedly used cruel means to deal with the plaintiff, a weak and helpless woman. If she does not seek legal relief, her life will inevitably be in danger. For the sake of survival, in addition to submitting the two injury reports for verification at the trial, she is suing in accordance with Article 293 of the Criminal Law, requesting that the case be brought to justice and punished as deserved, and that she be ordered to compensate for the corresponding medical expenses, etc. The court approved the statement and issued a ticket. This morning, Judge Shen Shumu came to the court to gather information. The plaintiff, Jiang Cuiling, and her agent, lawyer Chen Bingxing, were present to present the case, but the defendant, Sun Yunqing, was not present. The agent lawyer, Ni Zheng, was present and requested a postponement. Judge Shen ordered that the case be postponed for another hearing.

Cao Zhang's death was tragic

Shot and chopped into seven pieces 144

Cao Aliuh repays his mother

Encountered the murderer Pan Xiaodi

Cao Ren'an, a native of Tongzhou, is 26 years old and works as a rickshaw puller. He lives with his wife, Zuo, and his brother, Cao Aliuh, at No. 20 Yongxing Lane, Yongxing Road, Zhabei. On February 18th of the lunar calendar last year, Cao Zuo suddenly disappeared. After her husband, Ren'an, investigated in detail, he learned that she was seduced by his fellow villager Pan Xiaodi (25 years old, also a rickshaw puller) and fled to Dongsha, Nantongzhou, to live together. Therefore, his mother, Cao Zhang, went to Tongzhou alone in early May, intending to bring back his daughter-in-law, Zuo. Unexpectedly, on May 6th, Pan Xiaodi, together with two accomplices, brutally murdered her. First, Cao Zhang was shot to death with a pistol, and then her body was dismembered with a sharp knife and cut into seven pieces. Later, Ren'an heard about it in Shanghai and rushed to Tongzhou to report to the local authorities. In July, he captured two accomplices in the case, Hong Lianmazi and others, who confessed clearly and have already been executed by shooting. However, the murderer, Pan Xiaodi, has been at large and has not been arrested. Until about 6:00 AM on the 8th of this month, Pan Xiaodi was pulling a rickshaw from south to north on Xinnan Road when he was spotted by Cao Aliuh. He called the police, Nos. 1254 and 2886, who arrested Pan Xiaodi and brought him to the police station. Cao Aliuh was also temporarily detained as a key witness in the case. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stood up and presented the case. Cao Ren'an and Cao Aliuh also successively surrendered and explained the previous situation. When questioned, the defendant, Pan Xiaodi, confessed that the facts were falsely accused. After Cao Zuo disappeared, I and Ren'an searched everywhere. Later, I heard people say that she was abducted to Nantongzhou by my friend. I went to Tongzhou in May to search unsuccessfully and returned to Shanghai on the 13th. The plaintiffs should point out that I went to Tongzhou to inform them, and now they falsely accuse me of colluding to kill their mother. Please investigate clearly. After Judge Wu Tingqi verified the confession, he ordered Pan Xiaodi to be temporarily detained, pending the arrival of the official documents from Nantong County, before submitting the case for trial. Cao Aliuh was released in court.

Sun Wenbin

Extortion and Fraud Conviction 145

Appearance...Western Suit and Leather Shoes

Pocket...Three Copper Coins

A certain son of Zhu Cheng-cai of Ningbo, because of a previous crime, was sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment by the Hangzhou District Court. Sun Wenbin of Hangzhou learned of this matter and went to the Zhu family in Ningbo, telling them that he was very influential and that if they could spend several hundred gold coins, he could get their son released from prison. Zhu felt that he did not have such a large sum of money, so he thought of his cousin Xu Lichao, who opened the Xin Wan Xing Hotel at 1576 Wusong Road in Shanghai, who might be able to help. So he accompanied Sun to Shanghai on the Xin Jiang Tian steamboat on the 3rd of this month. When they arrived, Zhu suddenly discovered that a rattan suitcase had disappeared, containing twelve silver dollars and a letter from Xu Lichao instructing him to fetch his son Lian Gen's luggage (Lian Gen was an apprentice at Xin Wan Xing, but he no longer works there). Sun also disappeared at that time. Zhu immediately went to his cousin Xu Lichao and asked him to detain Sun if he came to collect the luggage under false pretenses. Then he returned to Ningbo. At half past nine in the morning, Sun indeed came to Xin Wan Xing with the letter to claim Lian Gen's luggage. Xu Lichao reported this to the Hongkou Police Station, and Chinese Detective Mao Yiwen and Detective Shen Dehui were ordered to arrest Sun and take him to the police station. Twenty-six cards were found on his person, printed with the words "Graduate of the Law Department of the Whampoa Central Political and Military Academy of Guangdong," "Prosecutor Sun Lie of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court Special Zone Court," and a certificate from the Recruitment Office of the Second Division of the National Government Garrison Army Zhejiang Special Zone, a badge from the Central Military Academy, and a badge from the Nanxun Railway No. 226. He was immediately taken into custody. The court clerk was also asked whether there was a person named Sun Lie in the court. The answer was that there was no such person. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Li Zhishan, the lawyer of the police station, stated the case and asked for a strict investigation. Zhu Cheng-cai and others then testified. The defendant confessed that Sun Lie was indeed another person, a friend of his, who was now serving in the military somewhere. All the cards and badges belonged to him. On the 5th of this month, he came to Shanghai from Ningbo and got separated from Zhu at the dock. Yesterday, he went to Xin Wan Xing to inquire whether Zhu had been there and was arrested. He denied stealing Zhu Cheng-cai's twelve silver dollars. After Judge Xiao Xiexun verified the confession, he sentenced Sun Wenbin to one year of imprisonment in court. The twenty-six cards were confiscated, and the badges and certificates were presented to the court. It is said that when Sun was arrested, he was dressed in a Western suit and leather shoes, but his pocket was empty, with only three copper coins.

Huo Yue'e

Accusing Her Divorced Husband 146

Accusing Husband of Stealing Clothes and Cash

Court Hearing This Morning

Huo Yue'e, a Cantonese woman currently residing at 162 Yuqingfang, North Sichuan Road, is 26 years old. In the eighteenth year of the Republic of China, she married Ding Lucheng, a graduate of Guanghua University who works as a clerk at the Dahua Electric Company on the upper floor of the Shuimingchang Wood Shop at the intersection of Sichuan Road and Beijing Road, through a matchmaker. Recently, Ding fell in love with a woman named Hui Zhen, which led to disagreements between the couple, eventually leading to divorce. Three days after the divorce, Ding took away all of Huo's clothes and other items. Huo then hired lawyer Xi Ya'fu to file a complaint with the Special District Court, requesting that he be punished for theft and that the items be returned. Her complaint stated that the plaintiff married the defendant in the eighteenth year of the Republic of China, and the relationship between the couple was very harmonious. However, the defendant was naturally lustful and, after marrying, continued to seek pleasure with prostitutes, becoming acquainted with Hui Zhen. He deliberately abandoned the plaintiff and often abused her. When she argued with him, the defendant relied on his financial power to hire a lawyer to send letters to lure her, forcing her to break off the marriage relationship with the defendant. Since she was ignorant and without the help of relatives and friends, she had no choice but to sign a separation agreement at the defendant's lawyer's office on July 10, with the defendant paying alimony of 650 yuan. He would first pay 200 yuan, and the remaining amount would be paid at 25 yuan per month. All of the plaintiff's clothes, boxes, and other items were to belong to the plaintiff. However, the defendant was heartless and listened to the slanders of his mistress, taking advantage of the plaintiff's isolation. On the afternoon of July 13, while she was out shopping, he came to her house and secretly stole a phonograph, thirty-two records, and a mineral leather suitcase. The tenants Guan Manli and her nanny witnessed this. The suitcase contained a gray squirrel cheongsam, a silk gauze cloak, a wool coat, a velvet-lined cheongsam, and a silk velvet-lined cheongsam, each one piece. The defendant had given her eighty silver dollars, and since the plaintiff was stranded in a foreign land with no relatives or close friends, the stolen clothing items were her daily wear, and the remaining eighty dollars was her only remaining money. Now that he had stolen everything, he was practically putting her to death. She has now filed a complaint with the Fifth Sub-station of the Public Security Bureau, and therefore files this complaint, requesting assistance in summoning the ruthless and unrighteous defendant to court and punishing him for the crime under Article 337 of the criminal law. The court approved the complaint and scheduled a court hearing for this morning (the 11th).

20th Anniversary of the Zhonghua Book Company 147

The Zhonghua Book Company was founded in the early years of the Republic of China. Now that it is the 20th anniversary, and it coincides with the 20th National Day of the Republic of China, a commemorative coupon event will be held for two months, from August 10th to October 9th. The details are as follows: (1) Types of coupons: (A) During the commemorative period, for every 5 jiao (half a dollar) in silver dollars spent on purchasing books published by Zhonghua Book Company, a book coupon worth 1 jiao will be given. For every 1 silver dollar spent, a book coupon worth 2 jiao will be given. (B) During the commemorative period, for every 1 silver dollar spent on purchasing instruments, stationery, pre-ordered books, special-priced books, pre-subscribed magazines, original Western books, and printed name cards from Zhonghua Book Company, a book coupon worth 1 jiao will be given. (2) The above coupon method is limited to cash purchases. More is given proportionately. No coupons will be given for purchases less than the specified amount or for account transactions. (3) Customers who purchase Zhonghua Book Company publications and pre-ordered books, special-priced books, and pre-subscribed magazines from bookstores in various places will be given book coupons by the bookstores in accordance with the preceding provisions. The issuing office will be responsible for redeeming the book coupons. (4) All prices are calculated in Shanghai standard silver dollars. Branches and counterparts in other places may add postage and remittance fees as appropriate. (5) For mail orders from other places, the date stamp affixed by the post office will be used as proof of the delivery date. All orders postmarked before the deadline of the commemoration will be given coupons. For non-mail orders, the date of receipt will be used as the basis. (6) Sold books, stationery, and other items will not be returned or exchanged. (7) No additional coupons will be given for redeeming coupons for books. (8) No coupons will be given for custom printing and purchasing machinery, lead type, and raw materials. (9) During the commemorative period, all library discount coupons issued by the company in the past will be temporarily suspended, and either the commemorative regulations will be followed, or the coupons will be honored, but no book coupons will be given.

Concession Telephone Numbers to be Changed 149

Due to Relocation to New Automatic Switching Room

The Jiangxi Road Telephone Company issued an important notice yesterday to inform users: For a considerable period in the past, the telephone lines of some users have been connected to two switching rooms, one is the old switching room, and the other is the new switching room. The user may not even know this. This is a necessary procedure in order to move thousands of telephone lines to the new switching room simultaneously in an instant. Now the time for the move is ripe, so there are already two places that will be switched from the old switching room, one is Bixun (users whose first digit of the phone number is 7), and the other is Huishan (users whose first digit of the phone number is 5). These two new automatic switching rooms will be put into practical use in the near future. The official date will be announced in the notice and in the newspapers. To avoid disappointment for users, please pay attention to the following point: Because of the merger of the two types of machines, there has been a slight obstacle. Therefore, during this relocation, there will be a risk of confusion when separating the two types of machines. However, our company is confident that all users will be delighted to see this relocation, as it is another step closer to a more perfect telephone service. Given the size of Shanghai, it is necessary to increase telephone zones. Therefore, many telephone numbers have been changed. Our company has a special request for all users: when calling numbers starting with 3, 4, 5, or 7, please check the changed number list first. The changed number list (attached) shows the numbers that have been changed after the telephone line relocation. Before the telephone line is relocated, do not use the new number. However, after the relocation, everyone must use the new number.

Wusong

Rickshaw License Donation Turmoil Settles 150

Yesterday, Licenses Were Issued in Accordance with Regulations

The details of the rickshaw license donation dispute in Wusong have been recorded in previous newspapers. Previously, the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau requested the municipal government to consider that rickshaw pullers are mostly poor people and cannot afford the fees. Therefore, a flexible method was determined, temporarily allowing them to pay half the donation, and increasing it after the city center area is expanded in the future. However, for the time being, they are only allowed to operate in the Wusong area, with a quota of 163 vehicles. However, there are currently about 200 rickshaws in Wusong, so the rickshaw pullers were panicked when they heard the news and sent representatives to petition the Eighth District Party Headquarters several times. At eight o'clock yesterday morning, all the rickshaws gathered in front of the vehicle affairs office on the outer road to wait for inspection and to receive licenses. The District Party Headquarters and the Seventh District Public Security Bureau feared that disputes would arise and sent personnel to the scene to take care of the situation and explain to the rickshaw pullers. The order was quite good at the time. The vehicle affairs office stipulated that each rickshaw puller could only receive one license, and a total of 154 licenses were issued. There were nine licenses remaining. However, there were more than 30 vehicles in the Baoshan area. Because there was a surplus, they were not issued. At the request of the rickshaw pullers, Director An agreed to find a way to increase the number in the shortest possible time. Therefore, this turmoil was settled.

Sino-Foreign Pharmacy

Su Renjie and Others Appeal Opens 151

Su Denies Being the Manager

The Sino-Foreign Pharmacy at 69 Guangdong Road was found to be selling prohibited drugs by Song Bingzheng, Bao Tan Zhang Shaoqing, Ding Yugao, etc. of the Anti-Narcotics Department of the General Patrol Room. They went to search the premises and seized morphine, cocaine, heroin, red pills, opium, etc., worth about 40,000 yuan, as well as a gas pistol. The manager of the store, Su Renjie, the accountant Rui Lai (i.e. Rui Lan), the owner Qiao Zixing (i.e. Qu Fengjie, the owner of Wanfeng Lumber Mill in Pudong), and the chief accountant Sun Chunsheng were arrested and handed over to the Special District Court. The court sentenced Su and Qiao to three years of imprisonment each and fined them 5,000 yuan. Wang Ruilan and Sun Chunsheng were sentenced to two years of imprisonment each and fined them 4,000 yuan. The prohibited items were confiscated. Su and the other four were not satisfied with the judgment and hired a lawyer to appeal to the Second Branch of the High Court. Yesterday morning, Song Yuan, the criminal court president of the High Court branch, together with Judges Du and Ye, held a hearing to question them. The patrol room was represented by lawyer Zhang Tianyin. Court President Song first asked Su Renjie if he was the manager of Sino-Foreign Pharmacy. Su replied that he was not. The manager's name was Zhang Changgui, and the accountant's name was Gao Ruyuan. He was a shop assistant in the retail department. On May 10th, Manager Zhang had to go to a friend's place for a drink and asked him to hand over two sample packages from the drawer when someone came to pick up samples. He then went out. At 11 o'clock, the detectives came and arrested him. Mr. Song then asked if he had confessed that morphine was 18 yuan per tael. He replied that this was a false confession, and that his real name was Su Chunlin, and Renjie was a pseudonym. The manager's monthly salary was over 100 yuan, while his monthly salary was only 29 yuan, which clearly showed that he was not the manager. Regarding this point, there was a salary book to prove it. When Wang Ruilan was questioned, he confessed that he was the one who managed the banknotes at the foreign account desk, with a monthly salary of 32 yuan. The matter of morphine was secretly operated by the manager, and he did not participate in it. Qiao Zixing confessed that he went to Sino-Foreign Pharmacy to visit his friend Zhang Changgui that day, and was arrested as soon as he entered the parlor. His real name was not Qu Fengjie, Qu was his former cohabitant. Court President Song asked Qiao if he had been sentenced to six months of imprisonment by the court in the tenth year of the Republic of China for selling drugs, and whether he had been imprisoned under the name of Qu Fengjie at that time. He replied that it was, but this fact was an injustice, and that he had opened a Wanfeng lumber mill in Pudong, which could be investigated. Sun Chunsheng confessed that he was doing transactions with Xia Jiasheng, a broker at Taixing No. 28 of the Gauze Exchange, and did not hold any position in Sino-Foreign Pharmacy. He was also visiting Zhang Changgui that day. After Court President Song verified the confessions, he ordered that the case be adjourned for further hearing.

Petition Submitted by the Songhu District Municipal Committee Regarding the Water Shortage 159

Chen Yaofu, a member of the Songhu District Municipal Committee, along with Yao Shuda, the executive director of the Songhu District Farmers' Association and the headmen of various "tu" (local administrative units) of the 30th "bao" (larger administrative unit), have submitted a petition stating that continuous torrential rains have dashed hopes for the autumn harvest. They earnestly request that the authorities be asked to conduct an on-site inspection to provide relief. The municipal committee has already prepared a document to submit to the Bureau of Social Affairs, requesting them to dispatch personnel for investigation. The content of the petition is as follows: This petition concerns the disaster caused by continuous torrential rains, leaving no hope for the autumn harvest. We submit this situation and earnestly request your review and approval, and that you send personnel to conduct an on-site inspection to devise relief measures.

According to the joint petition from the headmen Lu Yuanxiang and Zhu Shengwu, etc., of various "hei tu" within the 30th "bao" of the district: "We have observed that since the beginning of the 'Great Heat' solar term, continuous torrential rains have lasted for over ten days. River water has surged, and the bean crops in the fields have been soaked, causing the roots to rot. Weeds have proliferated, making it impossible to hoe or cultivate. Farmers are distressed and worried, all saying that disaster has already struck, and their cries of suffering fill the sky. Moreover, this year's spring harvest was also poor. If another famine occurs, it is unimaginable how we will survive. The headmen have witnessed the situation and know that disaster has struck, with no hope for the autumn harvest. We feel the pain deeply. Therefore, we specially submit this petition for your committee's review and approval, and request that it be forwarded to the Bureau of Social Affairs so they may quickly dispatch personnel to conduct an on-site inspection and devise methods for relief in advance. We await your orders with utmost urgency."

While we were preparing to submit this petition, we also received a letter from Yao Shuda, the executive director of the Songhu District Farmers' Association, stating: "The agricultural crops in our district are mainly cotton and beans. The 'Summer Solstice' and 'Slight Heat' solar terms are the time for cotton cultivation. However, due to continuous rainfall, the rivers have overflowed, flooding the plains by several feet. Cotton and bean crops have been submerged, and weeds have grown unchecked, signaling a water shortage. The national tax and people's livelihood depend on agricultural production. Now, due to the rain disaster, there is no hope for the autumn harvest. How will farmers maintain their livelihoods? As a farmer, Shuda, on behalf of farmers, specifically writes to you, respectfully requesting you to report to the government to seek a solution to this situation and provide relief to the people's livelihood."

Having received this information, we have learned that agricultural products in the district mainly consist of cotton and beans. Now, due to continuous torrential rains, the harvest is already hopeless. Based on the aforementioned circumstances, we should prepare a document to submit to your bureau, requesting you to quickly dispatch personnel to conduct an on-site inspection and devise relief measures to alleviate the people's livelihood. This is truly a matter of public benefit.

Over twenty polders, large and small, have been turned into a swamp. Houses have been swept away, and people have been displaced. Maintaining livelihoods is currently very difficult."

They also received a telegram from Cao Qingquan, a resident of the Haikouzhou Guangcheng Polder in Huaining County, Anhui, stating: "Since recently, our polder has experienced continuous heavy rains, causing mountain floods to break out and river tides to rise sharply, leading to the collapse of the polder dike and the destruction of countless houses. Food, livestock, and utensils have been swept away. Thousands of households of men, women, old, and young in the entire polder were unable to escape in time, resulting in many drownings. Now, we are without clothes or food, and our suffering is extreme."

Plan for the Municipal Construction of a National Goods Department Store 161

A Four-Story Steel-Framed Building

Located at the Old West Gate Triangle

Since the Shanghai Municipal National Goods Exhibition Hall moved to Zhonghua Road at the Xiaodongmen, it has been renovated and expanded, looking completely new. However, the building is still not large enough. Therefore, the hall decided to design and build its own grand new building. After finding the Old West Gate triangle, they prepared a plan, submitted it to Mayor Zhang and Director Pan for approval, and filed it with the Ministry of Interior. They are now actively planning and proceeding with the project. It is said that after completion, part of it will be used as the National Goods Exhibition Hall, and the rest will be an attached National Goods Department Store. The plan has been approved by the Municipal Council, allowing the land to be acquired for construction. The matter will be handled jointly by the four bureaus of Social Affairs, Public Works, Finance, and Land, together with the Municipal National Goods Exhibition Hall. Yesterday, a reporter from the Guowen News Agency inquired with each bureau and obtained the following plan:

Acquisition of Land: The triangle near the Chen Yingshi Memorial Pagoda at the West Gate, with a total area of slightly less than 3.3 mu (Chinese acres), is private land. The Land Bureau is currently surveying and purchasing it, and the purchase price is expected to be around 100,000 yuan. After the purchase, a five-story concrete steel-framed building will be constructed there, to be used as the Municipal National Goods Exhibition Hall and an attached department store.

Construction Costs: The Public Works Bureau estimates that the construction cost of the building is 1,200 taels of silver per "fang" (a unit of area). Excluding the area designated for road construction, the total land occupies 170 "fang," requiring a total construction cost of over 280,000 yuan. Including 80,000 yuan for elevators, water, electricity, sanitation, and roofing equipment, and 120,000 yuan for land prices and demolition costs, the total cost is estimated to be over 500,000 yuan. It is said that the funds have been designated by the Municipal Government to be allocated from the business tax revenue.

Internal Arrangement: The layout inside the building will be as follows: The fourth floor will be used for the exhibition hall's office and for displaying national goods. The remaining first, second, and third floors will be used as a department store. It is estimated that a total of 50 buildings can be constructed. In the future, national goods manufacturers will rent the premises to set up shops for business, and the hall will collect rent at its discretion. The building will also be equipped with two elevators. The entire building will also have its own power generation equipment for lighting. The latest methods will be used for fire prevention and sanitation equipment. Construction will begin in October of this year, and it is expected to be completed by the Double Tenth Festival (October 10th) next year at the latest.

Remarks from the Director: Dong Kerin, the director of the Municipal National Goods Exhibition Hall, said, "Recently, gold prices have soared, and everything has become expensive. During this period, promoting national goods is definitely the best opportunity. Although there is no shortage of organizations promoting national goods in Shanghai, there is still a lack of a liaison and guidance organization for reference in the city. The design of our hall's new building is for this purpose. Currently, the building design and the acquisition of land have been decided, and the required funds have also been approved by the Municipal Government, allocating 500,000 yuan from business tax revenue. The eastern part of the building will be four stories, and the western part will be five stories. In addition to the three floors dedicated to the department store and the fourth floor for the exhibition hall, a spacious auditorium will be arranged on the fifth floor on the west side. All construction will be carried out using the latest engineering methods. As soon as the Public Works Bureau has completed the drawings and submitted them to the Municipal Government for approval, construction will begin. In the future, with this organization promoting national goods in southern Shanghai, it will not only be easier for the public to understand the urgency of using national goods to save the country, but also the commercial activity in the West Gate area will become more prosperous."

The Taxpayers' Association Yesterday

Proposed Ten Issues to the Shanghai Municipal Council Suggesting Improvement of Municipal Administration 162

Requests a Deadline for Research and Implementation

Wang Xiaolai and Xu Wanqing, the chairman of the Chinese Ratepayers Association, sent a letter to Macnaghten, the chairman of the board of directors of the Shanghai Municipal Council, yesterday, regarding the issue of improving municipal administration. The letter stated, "Dear Sir, We have the following proposals that we request your attention and adoption by the chairman and all directors. We believe that municipal administration is evolving rather than static and should gradually improve with the times and the situation. What the residents like should be liked, and what the residents dislike should be disliked. The municipal administration of the Shanghai International Settlement has a history of nearly a century. With the evolution of the times and changes in the situation, there are many things that were suitable in the past but are not suitable now. If appropriate solutions that suit the times and the situation are not considered, it will not only cause unnecessary disputes but also hinder the improvement of residents' welfare. From the perspective of our association, the following issues should be addressed: (1) How to improve residents' knowledge of municipal administration; (2) How to establish a common representative body for Chinese and foreign residents to enable more effective cooperation on municipal facilities; (3) How to ensure that the expansion of the city's economy and the residents' economic capacity are mutually adapted; (4) How to ensure that residents are not unfairly burdened with city taxes; (5) How to ensure that land deeds are beneficial and without drawbacks; (6) How to ensure that matters such as interest rates on Chinese merchants' mortgages and pledges comply with Chinese law; (7) How to ensure that the four departments of public works, sanitation, firefighting, and taxation coordinate their intentions and facilitate residents in the issuance of notifications; (8) How to ensure that lower-level employees cannot or dare not engage in disreputable conduct by taking advantage of their positions; (9) How to legally resolve the issue of cross-border road construction; (10) Other issues related to the improvement of municipal administration. For the above suggestions, we sincerely hope that you will allow a period of one year for detailed research and the creation of an execution plan for adoption and implementation. In the opinion of our association, this task should be undertaken by municipal advisors. Our association believes that these suggestions are of great importance to the improvement of municipal administration. We are accordingly sending this letter, hoping that you will examine it carefully and uphold public interests."

Request to Waive National Goods Advertising Fees 163

Wang Shuxi and Four National Goods Organizations Sent a Telegram to the Organizing Committee of the National Games

Four National Goods Organizations Sent a Telegram to the Organizing Committee of the National Games

The China National Goods Maintenance Association, Promotion Association, Mechanical Union, and Factory Union held a joint meeting the other day and decided to send a telegram to the Organizing Committee of the National Games, requesting that the commercial areas and advertisements be nationalized and free of charge, and presenting methods. The original telegram stated, "To the Preparatory Committee of the National Games of the Capital: Your committee is devoted to promoting the national spirit and developing sports, making tireless efforts to organize and conduct the games. Your aims are lofty and your intentions profound, and we are deeply impressed. We, the undersigned, have decided at a joint meeting that, for the sake of promoting national glory, the commercial areas and all advertisements within the venue of your committee must be entirely nationalized. By taking advantage of this opportunity, you can give students from all over the country, overseas Chinese, and visiting people the opportunity to recognize national goods, arouse the concept of promoting national goods, and thereby develop industry, in line with the central government's seven sports work objectives. However, we have found that your committee's commercial area recruitment charter and advertising rules all have provisions for paying fees. The government has allocated 1.5 million yuan of national funds to cover the expenses of the National Games. How can these small fees compensate for the actual costs? You should consider that the national goods movement is related to the national economy and the people's livelihood, and grant a full exemption to support national goods publicity. The national goods sector should also uphold the spirit of promoting sports, cooperation, and mutual assistance. Each manufacturer should select high-quality products to display and demonstrate, and voluntarily sacrifice some products as prizes or gifts to encourage and reward outstanding achievements. We do not have any commercial intentions in this regard, but we dare not lag behind foreigners in promoting national goods. Otherwise, the very small income of your committee will only create opportunities for foreign goods publicity and have a very significant and profound impact on the future of national goods. We, the undersigned, uphold the duty of promoting national goods and are entrusted with the heavy responsibility by hundreds of factories. We are closely related to this matter and respectfully present our views. We jointly send this telegram to your committee, asking you to consider the infancy of the national goods industry and the importance of publicity opportunities. We earnestly request that you approve our request and waive all fees for commercial areas and advertisements, and assist in the implementation of the presentation of exhibits and gifts. This will be fortunate for national goods, and also fortunate for the national economy and the people's livelihood. We look forward to your reply in order to convene factories in Shanghai to discuss methods and actively proceed. We are eagerly awaiting your response. The China National Goods Maintenance Association, Shanghai Citizen National Goods Promotion Association, Shanghai National Goods Factory Federation, and Shanghai Mechanical National Goods Factory Federation jointly salute, [seal]."

New Fire Protection Engineering at the Continental Bank Warehouse 171

The Continental Bank has built a new warehouse on Suzhou River Road in Guangfu Road. It is a six-story concrete steel-frame structure with well-equipped internal facilities. The fire protection engineering is a new type of dry pipe system, which is free of water under normal circumstances to avoid the risk of freezing in cold weather. It was contracted by Gu Fali Foreign Firm at 137 Sichuan Road and has been completed. For the sake of safety, the Zhabei Fire Brigade Association conducted an on-site test at the warehouse on the afternoon of the 8th of this month. Led by the deputy chief of the third section, Zhang Deng, the section members carried over a dozen fire extinguishers and fire fighting equipment and tested them layer by layer. When they reached the roof, they simultaneously sprayed water using two canvas hoses. The water pressure was sufficient. Zhang and Deng were satisfied with the project. It is said that the Zhabei Fire Brigade Association consists entirely of volunteer members, who work so diligently. The future of fire protection in the Chinese community is truly commendable.
